We consider the following samples
\begin{enumerate}
\item USAF target (×2 zoom), see Sec. \ref{sec:usaf_x2}
\item USAF target (×12 zoom), see Sec. \ref{sec:usaf_x12}
\item Siemens star (×2 zoom), see Sec. \ref{sec:star_sector_x2}
\item Siemens star (×12 zoom), see Sec. \ref{sec:star_sector_x12}
\item Siemens star with linear variable filter, see Sec. \ref{sec:star_sector_linear}
\item Tomato slice (×2 zoom), see Sec. \ref{sec:tomato_slice_x2}
\item Tomato slice (×12 zoom), see Sec. \ref{sec:tomato_slice_x12}
\item STL10 cat, see Sec. \ref{sec:cat}
\item STL10 cat with linear variable filter, see Sec. \ref{sec:cat_linear}
\item STL10 horse, see Sec. \ref{sec:horse}
\end{enumerate}

We consider the following network
\begin{enumerate}
\item USAF target (×2 zoom), see \ref{sec:usaf_x2}
\item USAF target (×12 zoom), see \ref{sec:usaf_x12}
\item Siemens star (×2 zoom), see \ref{sec:star_sector_x2}
\item Siemens star (×12 zoom), see \ref{sec:star_sector_x12}
\item Siemens star with linear variable filter, see \ref{sec:star_sector_linear}
\item Tomato slice (×2 zoom), see \ref{sec:tomato_slice_x2}
\item Tomato slice (×12 zoom), see \ref{sec:tomato_slice_x12}
\item STL10 cat, see \ref{sec:cat}
\item STL10 cat with linear variable filter, see \ref{sec:cat_linear}
\item STL10 horse, see \ref{sec:horse}
\end{enumerate}
